\DoxyCodeLine{4121         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (n.le.6) then}

\DoxyCodeLine{4127               norm\_dd =  max(norm\_dd,abs(tn2(i)))}

\DoxyCodeLine{4130 }

\DoxyCodeLine{4153 }
